***заполонить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заполонить.html>заполони́ть</a> (24498)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">полони́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">polonítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заполонить.html>заполони́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zapolonítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">заполоня́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take prisoner, to take captive</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to captivate, to charm</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fill up (a space, a place)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">take captive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пленить.html>плени́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">plenítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">полони́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">polonítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полный.html>поло́н</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">polón</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">полоня́ник</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">polonjánik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">полоня́ничный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">polonjáničnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">полоня́ничек</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">polonjániček</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получить.html>получи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">polučítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***запоминание.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:запоминание.html>запомина́ние</a> (30221)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запоминать.html>запомина́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zapominátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запоминание.html>запомина́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zapominánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запоминание.html>запомина́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запоминание.html>запомина́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запоминание.html>запомина́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>memorization, memorizing</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запоминать.html>запомина́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zapominájuščij</span>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помнить.html>по́мнить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pómnitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***запор.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:запор.html>запо́р</a> (9736)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запор.html>запо́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zapór</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запор.html>запо́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запор.html>запо́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запор.html>запо́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>latch, lock</li>
<li>constipation</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***запорошить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:запорошить.html>запороши́ть</a> (19191)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пороши́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">porošítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запорошить.html>запороши́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaporošítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">запора́шивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">often  impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dust, to cover lightly, to cover with a thin layer <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of snow or dust</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гу</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:запорошить.html>запороши́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>сне́гом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dorógu <b>zaporošílo</b> snégom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the road was covered with a fine layer of snow</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to begin to fall lightly <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of snow</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пороши́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">porošítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">поро́ша</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poróša</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порошок.html>порошо́к</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">porošók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заправить.html>запра́вить</a> (10905)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>пра́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">právitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заправить.html>запра́вить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaprávitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заправлять.html>заправля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tuck in
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заправить.html>запра́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:брюки.html>брю́ки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сапог.html>сапоги́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaprávitʹ</b> brjúki v sapogí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tuck one's trousers [trouser bottoms] into one's boots</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заправить.html>запра́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кровать.html>крова́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaprávitʹ</b> krovátʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to do one's bed; tuck in the bed</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fill
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заправить.html>запра́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бак.html>бак</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:горючий.html>горю́чим</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaprávitʹ</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бак.html>bak</a> gorjúčim</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fill/fuel the tank; fill up</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to feed, to insert
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заправить.html>запра́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лента.html>ле́нту</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:пленка.html>плёнку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaprávitʹ</b> léntu/pljonku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to thread a tape/film</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заправить.html>запра́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:швейный.html>шве́йную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́ну</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:нитка.html>ни́ткой</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaprávitʹ</b> švéjnuju mašínu (nítkoj)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to thread in a sewing machine</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to dress <i>(with)</i>, to season <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заправить.html>запра́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:салат.html>сала́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:масло.html>ма́слом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уксус.html>у́ксусом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaprávitʹ</b> salát máslom i úksusom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dress the salad with oil and vinegar</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заправить.html>запра́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мука.html>муко́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaprávitʹ</b> mukój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to mix flour (into); thicken with flour</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заправить.html>запра́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:щи.html>щи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сметана.html>смета́ной</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaprávitʹ</b> šči smetánoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">add sour cream to the cabbage soup</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***заправка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заправка.html>запра́вка</a> (18045)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заправить.html>запра́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaprávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заправка.html>запра́вка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaprávka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заправка.html>запра́вки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заправка.html>запра́вки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заправка.html>запра́вок</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заправочный.html>запра́вочный</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cooking</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> seasoning, dressing</li>
<li>filling (with fuel)</li>
<li>gas station, petrol station</li></ol>

***заправлять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заправлять.html>заправля́ть</a> (15512)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заправить.html>запра́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaprávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заправлять.html>заправля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zapravljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заправить.html>запра́вить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tuck in
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заправлять.html>заправля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:брюки.html>брю́ки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сапог.html>сапоги́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zapravljátʹ</b> brjúki v sapogí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tuck one's trousers [trouser bottoms] into one's boots</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заправлять.html>заправля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кровать.html>крова́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zapravljátʹ</b> krovátʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to do one's bed; tuck in the bed</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fill
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заправлять.html>заправля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бак.html>бак</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:горючий.html>горю́чим</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zapravljátʹ</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бак.html>bak</a> gorjúčim</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fill/fuel the tank; fill up</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to feed, to insert
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заправлять.html>заправля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лента.html>ле́нту</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:пленка.html>плёнку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zapravljátʹ</b> léntu/pljonku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to thread a tape/film</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заправлять.html>заправля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:швейный.html>шве́йную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́ну</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:нитка.html>ни́ткой</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zapravljátʹ</b> švéjnuju mašínu (nítkoj)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to thread in a sewing machine</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to dress <i>(with)</i>, to season <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заправлять.html>заправля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:салат.html>сала́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:масло.html>ма́слом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уксус.html>у́ксусом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zapravljátʹ</b> salát máslom i úksusom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dress the salad with oil and vinegar</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заправлять.html>заправля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мука.html>муко́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zapravljátʹ</b> mukój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to mix flour (into); thicken with flour</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заправлять.html>заправля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:щи.html>щи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сметана.html>смета́ной</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zapravljátʹ</b> šči smetánoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">add sour cream to the cabbage soup</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to run, to rule, to boss, to call the shots
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заправлять.html>заправля́ть</a></b> чьи́ми-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>дела́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zapravljátʹ</b> čʹími-libo delámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run someone's affairs</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заправлять.html>заправля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всем</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zapravljátʹ</b> vsem</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run the show; rule the roost</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***запрашивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:запрашивать.html>запра́шивать</a> (19056)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запросить.html>запроси́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaprosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запрашивать.html>запра́шивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaprášivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запросить.html>запроси́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to inquire <i>(about, after)</i>, to request
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:запрашивать.html>запра́шивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сведение.html>све́дения</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaprášivatʹ</b> svédenija u kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to request information from smb</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:запрашивать.html>запра́шивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:предложение.html>предложе́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaprášivatʹ</b> predložénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to invite offers</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to request information <i>(from)</i>, to inquire <i>(of)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:запрашивать.html>запра́шивать</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:письменный.html>пи́сьменной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рме</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaprášivatʹ</b> kovó-libo v písʹmennoj fórme</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to send a written request for information</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to charge <i>(price)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:запрашивать.html>запра́шивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слишком.html>сли́шком</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорогой.html>до́рого</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> кого́-либо)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaprášivatʹ</b> slíškom dórogo (s kovó-libo)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ask too high a price (from); overcharge</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to call, to request
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:запрашивать.html>запра́шивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ввод.html>ввод</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:данный.html>да́нных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пользователь.html>по́льзователя</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaprášivatʹ</b> vvod dánnyx u pólʹzovatelja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to prompt the user for data input</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:запрашивать.html>запра́шивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:доступ.html>до́ступ</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaprášivatʹ</b> dóstup (k)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to seek/request access (to)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
